***drijfveer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:drijfveer.html>drijfveer</a> (25837)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drijven.html>drijven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drive, move</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veer.html>veer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">spring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Triebfeder</i>. From the second <a href = vnd.unilang:halve.html>halve</a> of the 18th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:drijfzand.html>drijfzand</a> (19891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drijven.html>drijven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drift</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zand.html>zand</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drijfzand.html>drijfzand</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> quicksand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a> in <b><a href = vnd.unilang:drijfzand.html>drijfzand</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:terecht.html>terecht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wist.html>wist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeite.html>moeite</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eruit.html>eruit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bevrijden.html>bevrijden</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He landed in <b>quicksand</b> and extricated himself from it only with difficulty.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a treacherous, tricky danger or risk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bezig.html>bezig</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:drijfzand.html>drijfzand</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> stagflatie <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> verzeilen.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The economy <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sliding.html>sliding</a> off into the <b>quagmire</b> of stagflation.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:drijven.html>drijven</a> (3967)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">driven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">drīvan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*drībaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰreybʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drive, push</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dril.html>dril</a> (76283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Likely borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">drill</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">drill</i> (see the oldest quotation), perhaps from an African language.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:drillen.html>drillen</a> (43873)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:drillen.html>drillen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thrillen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þriljaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ter-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">through, <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">thrill</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drillen.html>drillen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make vibrate, as with a pneumatic drill</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to operate a pneumatic drill</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drill, instruct by arduous exercise, notably in military context or style</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:domineer.html>domineer</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dringen.html>dringen</a> (6228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dringen.html>dringen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thringan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þrinhwaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dringen.html>dringen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press, push (into a tight space, a crowd etc)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to insist</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to force entry</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be short in supply (of time, etc)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tijd.html>tijd</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dringt.html>dringt</a></b></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">time <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> short</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:drinkgelag.html>drinkgelag</a> (76282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drinken.html>drinken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gelag.html>gelag</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drinkgelag.html>drinkgelag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drinkgelag.html>drinkgelagen</a></b>)

***drizzle.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a> (107368)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps a back-formation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dryseling</i>, a dissimilated variant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">drysning</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a falling of dew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">drysnan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to extinguish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">drēosan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fall, to decline</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, making it cognate to modern English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">droze</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">drowse</i>. Compare also dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">drösla</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">drizzles</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">drizzling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">drizzled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To rain lightly.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> planned a picnic for <a href = vnd.unilang:joe.html>Joe</a>'s birthday, but it ended up <b>drizzling</b> all day.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive, intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To shed slowly in minute <a href = vnd.unilang:drops.html>drops</a> or particles.
<ul><li><b>1579</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edmund_Spenser" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edmund Spenser">Edmund Spenser</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Shepheardes_Calender" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Shepheardes Calender">The Shepheardes Calender</a>,</i> London, Januarye, Aegloga <a href = vnd.unilang:prima.html>prima</a>,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://name.umdl.umich.edu/A12782.0001.001">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>And from mine <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> the <b>drizling</b> teares descend,</dd>
<dd>As on your boughes the ysicles depend.</dd></dl></li>
<li><i>c.</i> <b>1594</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romeo_and_Juliet" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Romeo and Juliet"><a href = vnd.unilang:romeo.html>Romeo</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:juliet.html>Juliet</a></a>,</i> Act III, Scene 5,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.opensourceshakespeare.org/views/plays/play_view.php?WorkID=romeojulietamp;Scope=entireamp;pleasewait=1amp;msg=pl">[2]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>When the sun <a href = vnd.unilang:sets.html>sets</a>, the air doth <b><a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a></b> dew;</dd>
<dd>But for the sunset of my brother’s son</dd>
<dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:rains.html>rains</a> downright.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To pour slowly and evenly, especially oil or honey in cooking.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The recipe says to toss the salad and then <b><a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a></b> olive oil on it.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cooking<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cover by pouring in this manner.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The recipe says to toss the salad and then <b><a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a></b> it in olive oil.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To urinate. <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> add an example for this sense?)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To carry out parfilage, the process of unravelling.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">drizzles</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Light rain.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> weather</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Very small, numerous, and uniformly dispersed water <a href = vnd.unilang:drops.html>drops</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mist.html>mist</a>, or sprinkle. Unlike fog droplets, <a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a> falls to the ground.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">No longer pouring, the rain outside slowed down to a faint <b><a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a></b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Water.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>Stop</a> drinking all of my <b><a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a></b>!</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">baking</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cake onto which icing, honey or syrup <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> drizzled in an artistic manner.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by <a href = vnd.unilang:felicity.html>Felicity</a> Cloake and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>Drizzle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not normally good news. Not when it's falling from the sky, not when it's replacing a decent helping of sauce, and especially not when it's found on a menu in close proximity to the <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> "balsamic vinegar". Deliciously sticky, sweet and sour lemon <b><a href = vnd.unilang:drizzle.html>drizzle</a></b> cake <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the one, and very honourable, exception.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:jules.html>Jules</a> Stanbridge,  <cite>Sugar and Spice</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a> of the day <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> spent trying to concentrate on ingredient <a href = vnd.unilang:labels.html>labels</a>, ordering supplies, baking some fairy <a href = vnd.unilang:cakes.html>cakes</a> for a <a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a> party and two lemon <b>drizzles</b>, one for a new <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a> and one for an old dear's birthday.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body> 
***droef.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:droef.html>droef</a> (45593)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:droeve.html>droeve</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">droue</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*drōvi</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*druovi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*drōbuz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">turbid</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">droff</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">trüb</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>sad, miserable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>Jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maakt.html>maakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:droef.html>droef</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You make <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <b>sad</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***droefenis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:droefenis.html>droefenis</a> (33441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droef.html>droef</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droefenis.html>droefenis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droefenis.html>droefenissen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droefenis.html>droefenisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sadness</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:droefenis.html>droefenis</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>  <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>

***drogreden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:drogreden.html>drogreden</a> (107365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">drog</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">falsehood; deceit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reden.html>reden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">reasoning; reason</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drogreden.html>drogreden</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drogredenen.html>drogredenen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drogreden.html>drogredentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sophism, an argument that <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> sense by itself but does not logically support the assertion it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> meant to prove, such as a non sequitur</li></ol>

vnd.unilang:niet.html>Niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> degradatiekandidaat”, <a href = vnd.unilang:stelde.html>stelde</a> VVV-trainer André Wetzel <a href = vnd.unilang:tevreden.html>tevreden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a>. <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dromer.html>dromer</a> (12858)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">drômere</i>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dromer.html>dromer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dromers.html>dromers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dromer.html>dromertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A dreamer, who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> (a) dream(s)</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:dronken.html>dronken</a> (985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:dronken.html>dronken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">drunkan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*drunkanaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***droogte.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:droogte.html>droogte</a> (13949)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">droochte</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droog.html>droog</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-te</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droogte.html>droogte</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droogten.html>droogten</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droogtes.html>droogtes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>drought</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:droomhuis.html>droomhuis</a> (23863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droom.html>droom</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dream</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droomhuis.html>droomhuis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droomhuis.html>droomhuizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:droomhuis.html>droomhuisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">dream house</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">ideal house</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">drove</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>

</p>
<ol><li>A person who <a href = vnd.unilang:drives.html>drives</a> animals, especially cattle or sheep, <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> long <a href = vnd.unilang:distances.html>distances</a>.
<ul><li><b>1599</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Much_Ado_About_Nothing" class="extiw" title="w:Much Ado About Nothing">Much Ado About Nothing</a></i>, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Much_Ado_About_Nothing_(Shakespeare)" class="extiw" title="s:Much Ado About Nothing (Shakespeare)">Act 2 Scene 1</a>
<dl><dd>Why, that's <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> like an honest <b>drovier</b>: so they sell <a href = vnd.unilang:bullocks.html>bullocks</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1893</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/W._S._Gilbert" class="extiw" title="w:W. S. Gilbert">W. S. <a href = vnd.unilang:gilbert.html>Gilbert</a></a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Utopia,_Limited" class="extiw" title="w:Utopia, Limited">Utopia, Limited</a></i>, Act 1
<dl><dd>Daily driven / (Wife as <a href = vnd.unilang:drover.html>drover</a>) / Ill you've thriven-- / Ne'<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> in clover.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">druc</i>. <p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:druk.html>druk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drukken.html>drukken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drukje.html>drukje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

</p>
<ol><li>busy, crowded, hectic (of a place)</li>

<li>restless, uneasy</li>

***drukken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:drukken.html>drukken</a> (3312)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">drucken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*thrucken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þrukkijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drukken.html>drukken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:drummer.html>drummer</a></i>.
